## 1. framing/framing.go

```go
// Package framing implements MLS Message Framing according to RFC 9420 §6.
//
// This package provides:
//   - PublicMessage (plaintext, signed)
//   - PrivateMessage (encrypted)
//   - FramedContent structure
//   - Sender types
//   - Content types (Application, Proposal, Commit)
//   - Wire format handling
package framing

import (
	"fmt"

	"github.com/openmls/go/ciphersuite"
	"github.com/openmls/go/group"
	"github.com/openmls/go/internal/tls"
)

// WireFormat identifies the type of MLS message on the wire.
type WireFormat uint16

const (
	WireFormatPublicMessage  WireFormat = 0x0001 // mls_public_message
	WireFormatPrivateMessage WireFormat = 0x0002 // mls_private_message
	WireFormatWelcome        WireFormat = 0x0003 // mls_welcome
	WireFormatGroupInfo      WireFormat = 0x0004 // mls_group_info
	WireFormatKeyPackage     WireFormat = 0x0005 // mls_key_package
)

// ContentType identifies the type of content within a message.
type ContentType uint8

const (
	ContentTypeApplication ContentType = 0x01 // Application data
	ContentTypeProposal    ContentType = 0x02 // Proposal message
	ContentTypeCommit      ContentType = 0x03 // Commit message
)

// Sender identifies who sent a message (RFC 9420 §6).
//
//	struct {
//	    SenderType sender_type;
//	    select (Sender.sender_type) {
//	        case member:        uint32 leaf_index;
//	        case external:      uint32 sender_index;
//	        case new_member:    struct{};
//	    };
//	} Sender;
type Sender struct {
	Type SenderType
	// For Member sender
	LeafIndex group.LeafNodeIndex
	// For External sender
	SenderIndex uint32
}

// SenderType identifies the type of sender.
type SenderType uint8

const (
	SenderTypeMember         SenderType = 0x01 // Group member
	SenderTypeExternal       SenderType = 0x02 // External sender
	SenderTypeNewMemberProposal SenderType = 0x03 // New member (external proposal)
	SenderTypeNewMemberCommit   SenderType = 0x04 // New member (external commit)
)

// IsMember returns true if the sender is a group member.
func (s *Sender) IsMember() bool {
	return s.Type == SenderTypeMember
}

// IsExternal returns true if the sender is external.
func (s *Sender) IsExternal() bool {
	return s.Type == SenderTypeExternal
}

// IsNewMember returns true if the sender is a new member.
func (s *Sender) IsNewMember() bool {
	return s.Type == SenderTypeNewMemberProposal || s.Type == SenderTypeNewMemberCommit
}

// NewMemberSender creates a member sender.
func NewMemberSender(leafIndex group.LeafNodeIndex) *Sender {
	return &Sender{
		Type:      SenderTypeMember,
		LeafIndex: leafIndex,
	}
}

// NewExternalSender creates an external sender.
func NewExternalSender(senderIndex uint32) *Sender {
	return &Sender{
		Type:        SenderTypeExternal,
		SenderIndex: senderIndex,
	}
}

// NewNewMemberProposalSender creates a new member proposal sender.
func NewNewMemberProposalSender() *Sender {
	return &Sender{Type: SenderTypeNewMemberProposal}
}

// NewNewMemberCommitSender creates a new member commit sender.
func NewNewMemberCommitSender() *Sender {
	return &Sender{Type: SenderTypeNewMemberCommit}
}

// Marshal serializes the Sender to TLS format.
func (s *Sender) Marshal() []byte {
	w := tls.NewWriter()
	w.WriteUint8(uint8(s.Type))

	switch s.Type {
	case SenderTypeMember:
		w.WriteUint32(s.LeafIndex.AsUint32())
	case SenderTypeExternal:
		w.WriteUint32(s.SenderIndex)
	// NewMember types have no additional data
	}

	return w.Bytes()
}

// UnmarshalSender deserializes a Sender from TLS format.
func UnmarshalSender(data []byte) (*Sender, error) {
	r := tls.NewReader(data)

	senderType, err := r.ReadUint8()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("reading sender type: %w", err)
	}

	sender := &Sender{Type: SenderType(senderType)}

	switch sender.Type {
	case SenderTypeMember:
		leafIndex, err := r.ReadUint32()
		if err != nil {
			return nil, fmt.Errorf("reading leaf index: %w", err)
		}
		sender.LeafIndex = group.NewLeafNodeIndex(leafIndex)

	case SenderTypeExternal:
		senderIndex, err := r.ReadUint32()
		if err != nil {
			return nil, fmt.Errorf("reading sender index: %w", err)
		}
		sender.SenderIndex = senderIndex
	}

	return sender, nil
}
```

## 2. framing/framed_content.go

```go
package framing

import (
	"fmt"

	"github.com/openmls/go/group"
	"github.com/openmls/go/internal/tls"
)

// FramedContent represents the content of an MLS message (RFC 9420 §6).
//
//	struct {
//	    opaque group_id<V>;
//	    uint64 epoch;
//	    Sender sender;
//	    opaque authenticated_data<V>;
//	    ContentType content_type;
//	    select (FramedContent.content_type) {
//	        case application:  opaque application_data<V>;
//	        case proposal:     Proposal proposal;
//	        case commit:       Commit commit;
//	    };
//	} FramedContent;
type FramedContent struct {
	GroupID           *group.GroupID
	Epoch             group.GroupEpoch
	Sender            *Sender
	AuthenticatedData []byte
	ContentType       ContentType
	Body              FramedContentBody
}

// FramedContentBody represents the body of framed content.
type FramedContentBody struct {
	// Only one of these should be set
	ApplicationData []byte
	Proposal        *group.Proposal
	Commit          *group.Commit
}

// NewApplicationContent creates application data content.
func NewApplicationContent(data []byte) *FramedContentBody {
	return &FramedContentBody{ApplicationData: data}
}

// NewProposalContent creates proposal content.
func NewProposalContent(proposal *group.Proposal) *FramedContentBody {
	return &FramedContentBody{Proposal: proposal}
}

// NewCommitContent creates commit content.
func NewCommitContent(commit *group.Commit) *FramedContentBody {
	return &FramedContentBody{Commit: commit}
}

// Marshal serializes the FramedContent to TLS format.
func (fc *FramedContent) Marshal() []byte {
	w := tls.NewWriter()

	w.WriteVLBytes(fc.GroupID.AsSlice())
	w.WriteUint64(fc.Epoch.AsUint64())
	w.WriteRaw(fc.Sender.Marshal())
	w.WriteVLBytes(fc.AuthenticatedData)
	w.WriteUint8(uint8(fc.ContentType))

	// Write body based on content type
	switch fc.ContentType {
	case ContentTypeApplication:
		w.WriteVLBytes(fc.Body.ApplicationData)
	case ContentTypeProposal:
		// Serialize proposal
		// TODO: Implement proper proposal serialization
		w.WriteVLBytes([]byte{})
	case ContentTypeCommit:
		// Serialize commit
		w.WriteVLBytes(fc.Body.Commit.Marshal())
	}

	return w.Bytes()
}

// UnmarshalFramedContent deserializes a FramedContent from TLS format.
func UnmarshalFramedContent(data []byte) (*FramedContent, error) {
	r := tls.NewReader(data)

	groupID, err := r.ReadVLBytes()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("reading group_id: %w", err)
	}

	epoch, err := r.ReadUint64()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("reading epoch: %w", err)
	}

	// Read sender (variable length, need to parse it)
	senderData := r.BytesAfterPosition()
	sender, err := UnmarshalSender(senderData)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("reading sender: %w", err)
	}
	// Skip sender bytes (approximate)
	r.Skip(len(sender.Marshal()))

	authData, err := r.ReadVLBytes()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("reading authenticated_data: %w", err)
	}

	contentTypeByte, err := r.ReadUint8()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("reading content_type: %w", err)
	}
	contentType := ContentType(contentTypeByte)

	fc := &FramedContent{
		GroupID:           group.NewGroupID(groupID),
		Epoch:             group.NewGroupEpoch(epoch),
		Sender:            sender,
		AuthenticatedData: authData,
		ContentType:       contentType,
	}

	// Read body based on content type
	bodyData, err := r.ReadVLBytes()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("reading body: %w", err)
	}

	switch contentType {
	case ContentTypeApplication:
		fc.Body = FramedContentBody{ApplicationData: bodyData}
	case ContentTypeProposal:
		// TODO: Deserialize proposal
		fc.Body = FramedContentBody{}
	case ContentTypeCommit:
		commit, err := group.UnmarshalCommit(bodyData)
		if err != nil {
			return nil, fmt.Errorf("unmarshaling commit: %w", err)
		}
		fc.Body = FramedContentBody{Commit: commit}
	}

	return fc, nil
}
```

## 3. framing/public_message.go

```go
package framing

import (
	"fmt"

	"github.com/openmls/go/ciphersuite"
	"github.com/openmls/go/internal/tls"
)

// PublicMessage represents a signed, unencrypted MLS message (RFC 9420 §6.2).
//
//	struct {
//	    WireFormat wire_format = mls_public_message;
//	    FramedContent content;
//	    FramedContentAuthData auth;
//	    opaque signature<V>;
//	    optional<MembershipTag> membership_tag;
//	} PublicMessage;
type PublicMessage struct {
	Content        *FramedContent
	Signature      *ciphersuite.Signature
	MembershipTag  []byte // Optional, only for member messages
}

// FramedContentAuthData contains authentication data for framed content.
type FramedContentAuthData struct {
	Signature      *ciphersuite.Signature
	ConfirmationTag []byte // Only for Commit messages
}

// NewPublicMessage creates a new public message.
func NewPublicMessage(content *FramedContent) *PublicMessage {
	return &PublicMessage{
		Content: content,
	}
}

// SetSignature sets the signature on the public message.
func (pm *PublicMessage) SetSignature(sig *ciphersuite.Signature) {
	pm.Signature = sig
}

// SetMembershipTag sets the membership tag (for member messages).
func (pm *PublicMessage) SetMembershipTag(tag []byte) {
	pm.MembershipTag = tag
}

// Marshal serializes the PublicMessage to TLS format.
func (pm *PublicMessage) Marshal() []byte {
	w := tls.NewWriter()

	// Wire format
	w.WriteUint16(uint16(WireFormatPublicMessage))

	// Content
	w.WriteRaw(pm.Content.Marshal())

	// Signature
	if pm.Signature != nil {
		w.WriteVLBytes(pm.Signature.AsSlice())
	} else {
		w.WriteVLBytes([]byte{})
	}

	// Membership tag (optional)
	if pm.MembershipTag != nil {
		w.WriteUint8(1) // present
		w.WriteVLBytes(pm.MembershipTag)
	} else {
		w.WriteUint8(0) // not present
	}

	return w.Bytes()
}

// UnmarshalPublicMessage deserializes a PublicMessage from TLS format.
func UnmarshalPublicMessage(data []byte) (*PublicMessage, error) {
	r := tls.NewReader(data)

	// Read wire format
	wireFormat, err := r.ReadUint16()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("reading wire format: %w", err)
	}

	if WireFormat(wireFormat) != WireFormatPublicMessage {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("unexpected wire format: %d", wireFormat)
	}

	// Read content (variable length)
	contentData, err := r.ReadVLBytes()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("reading content: %w", err)
	}

	content, err := UnmarshalFramedContent(contentData)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("unmarshaling content: %w", err)
	}

	pm := &PublicMessage{Content: content}

	// Read signature
	sigData, err := r.ReadVLBytes()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("reading signature: %w", err)
	}

	if len(sigData) > 0 {
		pm.Signature = ciphersuite.NewSignature(sigData)
	}

	// Read optional membership tag
	present, err := r.ReadUint8()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("reading membership tag presence: %w", err)
	}

	if present == 1 {
		tag, err := r.ReadVLBytes()
		if err != nil {
			return nil, fmt.Errorf("reading membership tag: %w", err)
		}
		pm.MembershipTag = tag
	}

	return pm, nil
}

// VerifySignature verifies the signature on the public message.
func (pm *PublicMessage) VerifySignature(publicKey *ciphersuite.OpenMlsSignaturePublicKey) error {
	if pm.Signature == nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("no signature present")
	}

	// Serialize content for verification
	contentBytes := pm.Content.Marshal()

	// Verify
	return publicKey.Verify(contentBytes, pm.Signature)
}

// ComputeMembershipTag computes the membership tag for a member message.
func (pm *PublicMessage) ComputeMembershipTag(membershipKey *ciphersuite.Secret) ([]byte, error) {
	// MAC over the message (without the tag itself)
	// membership_tag = MAC(membership_key, PublicMessageTBS)
	tbs := pm.marshalTBS()

	mac, err := membershipKey.Hmac(tbs)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("computing MAC: %w", err)
	}

	return mac, nil
}

// marshalTBS marshals the message for signature/MAC computation (To Be Signed).
func (pm *PublicMessage) marshalTBS() []byte {
	w := tls.NewWriter()

	// Wire format
	w.WriteUint16(uint16(WireFormatPublicMessage))

	// Content
	w.WriteRaw(pm.Content.Marshal())

	return w.Bytes()
}

// ConfirmedTranscriptHashInput computes the input for the confirmed transcript hash.
func (pm *PublicMessage) ConfirmedTranscriptHashInput() []byte {
	return pm.marshalTBS()
}

// InterimTranscriptHashInput computes the input for the interim transcript hash.
func (pm *PublicMessage) InterimTranscriptHashInput(confirmationTag []byte) []byte {
	w := tls.NewWriter()

	// Wire format
	w.WriteUint16(uint16(WireFormatPublicMessage))

	// Content
	w.WriteRaw(pm.Content.Marshal())

	// Signature
	if pm.Signature != nil {
		w.WriteVLBytes(pm.Signature.AsSlice())
	} else {
		w.WriteVLBytes([]byte{})
	}

	// Confirmation tag
	w.WriteVLBytes(confirmationTag)

	return w.Bytes()
}
```

## 4. framing/private_message.go

```go
package framing

import (
	"crypto/aes"
	"crypto/cipher"
	"encoding/binary"
	"fmt"

	"github.com/openmls/go/ciphersuite"
	"github.com/openmls/go/group"
	"github.com/openmls/go/internal/tls"
)

// PrivateMessage represents an encrypted MLS message (RFC 9420 §6.3).
//
//	struct {
//	    WireFormat wire_format = mls_private_message;
//	    opaque group_id<V>;
//	    uint64 epoch;
//	    ContentType content_type;
//	    opaque authenticated_data<V>;
//	    opaque encrypted_sender_data<V>;
//	    opaque ciphertext<V>;
//	} PrivateMessage;
type PrivateMessage struct {
	GroupID           *group.GroupID
	Epoch             group.GroupEpoch
	ContentType       ContentType
	AuthenticatedData []byte
	EncryptedSenderData []byte
	Ciphertext        []byte
}

// SenderData contains information about the sender (encrypted in PrivateMessage).
//
//	struct {
//	    uint32 leaf_index;
//	    uint32 generation;
//	    opaque reuse_guard[4];
//	} SenderData;
type SenderData struct {
	LeafIndex  group.LeafNodeIndex
	Generation uint32
	ReuseGuard [4]byte
}

// NewPrivateMessage creates a new private message.
func NewPrivateMessage(groupID *group.GroupID, epoch group.GroupEpoch, contentType ContentType) *PrivateMessage {
	return &PrivateMessage{
		GroupID:     groupID,
		Epoch:       epoch,
		ContentType: contentType,
	}
}

// SetCiphertext sets the encrypted content.
func (pm *PrivateMessage) SetCiphertext(ciphertext []byte) {
	pm.Ciphertext = ciphertext
}

// SetEncryptedSenderData sets the encrypted sender data.
func (pm *PrivateMessage) SetEncryptedSenderData(data []byte) {
	pm.EncryptedSenderData = data
}

// SetAuthenticatedData sets the authenticated data (AAD).
func (pm *PrivateMessage) SetAuthenticatedData(data []byte) {
	pm.AuthenticatedData = data
}

// Marshal serializes the PrivateMessage to TLS format.
func (pm *PrivateMessage) Marshal() []byte {
	w := tls.NewWriter()

	// Wire format
	w.WriteUint16(uint16(WireFormatPrivateMessage))

	// Group ID
	w.WriteVLBytes(pm.GroupID.AsSlice())

	// Epoch
	w.WriteUint64(pm.Epoch.AsUint64())

	// Content type
	w.WriteUint8(uint8(pm.ContentType))

	// Authenticated data
	w.WriteVLBytes(pm.AuthenticatedData)

	// Encrypted sender data
	w.WriteVLBytes(pm.EncryptedSenderData)

	// Ciphertext
	w.WriteVLBytes(pm.Ciphertext)

	return w.Bytes()
}

// UnmarshalPrivateMessage deserializes a PrivateMessage from TLS format.
func UnmarshalPrivateMessage(data []byte) (*PrivateMessage, error) {
	r := tls.NewReader(data)

	// Read wire format
	wireFormat, err := r.ReadUint16()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("reading wire format: %w", err)
	}

	if WireFormat(wireFormat) != WireFormatPrivateMessage {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("unexpected wire format: %d", wireFormat)
	}

	// Group ID
	groupID, err := r.ReadVLBytes()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("reading group_id: %w", err)
	}

	// Epoch
	epoch, err := r.ReadUint64()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("reading epoch: %w", err)
	}

	// Content type
	contentTypeByte, err := r.ReadUint8()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("reading content_type: %w", err)
	}

	// Authenticated data
	authData, err := r.ReadVLBytes()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("reading authenticated_data: %w", err)
	}

	// Encrypted sender data
	encSenderData, err := r.ReadVLBytes()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("reading encrypted_sender_data: %w", err)
	}

	// Ciphertext
	ciphertext, err := r.ReadVLBytes()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("reading ciphertext: %w", err)
	}

	return &PrivateMessage{
		GroupID:             group.NewGroupID(groupID),
		Epoch:               group.NewGroupEpoch(epoch),
		ContentType:         ContentType(contentTypeByte),
		AuthenticatedData:   authData,
		EncryptedSenderData: encSenderData,
		Ciphertext:          ciphertext,
	}, nil
}

// EncryptContent encrypts framed content for a private message.
//
// Uses the secret tree to derive keys for encryption.
func (pm *PrivateMessage) EncryptContent(
	content *FramedContent,
	senderData *SenderData,
	senderDataSecret *ciphersuite.Secret,
	encryptionSecret *ciphersuite.Secret,
) error {
	// Serialize content
	contentBytes := content.Marshal()

	// Derive keys from secret tree
	// TODO: Implement proper secret tree key derivation
	nonce := make([]byte, 12)
	key := make([]byte, 16)

	// Encrypt sender data first
	senderDataBytes := pm.marshalSenderData(senderData)
	encryptedSenderData, err := pm.encryptSenderData(senderDataBytes, senderDataSecret)
	if err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("encrypting sender data: %w", err)
	}
	pm.EncryptedSenderData = encryptedSenderData

	// Encrypt content
	aad := pm.computeAAD()
	ciphertext, err := pm.encryptWithAESGCM(contentBytes, key, nonce, aad)
	if err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("encrypting content: %w", err)
	}
	pm.Ciphertext = ciphertext

	return nil
}

// DecryptContent decrypts the content of a private message.
func (pm *PrivateMessage) DecryptContent(
	senderDataSecret *ciphersuite.Secret,
	encryptionSecret *ciphersuite.Secret,
) (*FramedContent, *SenderData, error) {
	// Decrypt sender data
	senderDataBytes, err := pm.decryptSenderData(pm.EncryptedSenderData, senderDataSecret)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, nil, fmt.Errorf("decrypting sender data: %w", err)
	}

	senderData, err := pm.unmarshalSenderData(senderDataBytes)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, nil, fmt.Errorf("unmarshaling sender data: %w", err)
	}

	// Derive keys from secret tree using sender data
	// TODO: Implement proper secret tree key derivation
	nonce := make([]byte, 12)
	key := make([]byte, 16)

	// Decrypt content
	aad := pm.computeAAD()
	contentBytes, err := pm.decryptWithAESGCM(pm.Ciphertext, key, nonce, aad)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, nil, fmt.Errorf("decrypting content: %w", err)
	}

	content, err := UnmarshalFramedContent(contentBytes)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, nil, fmt.Errorf("unmarshaling content: %w", err)
	}

	return content, senderData, nil
}

// marshalSenderData serializes sender data.
func (pm *PrivateMessage) marshalSenderData(sd *SenderData) []byte {
	w := tls.NewWriter()
	w.WriteUint32(sd.LeafIndex.AsUint32())
	w.WriteUint32(sd.Generation)
	w.WriteRaw(sd.ReuseGuard[:])
	return w.Bytes()
}

// unmarshalSenderData deserializes sender data.
func (pm *PrivateMessage) unmarshalSenderData(data []byte) (*SenderData, error) {
	if len(data) < 12 {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("sender data too short")
	}

	sd := &SenderData{
		LeafIndex:  group.NewLeafNodeIndex(binary.BigEndian.Uint32(data[0:4])),
		Generation: binary.BigEndian.Uint32(data[4:8]),
	}
	copy(sd.ReuseGuard[:], data[8:12])

	return sd, nil
}

// encryptSenderData encrypts sender data using sender_data_secret.
func (pm *PrivateMessage) encryptSenderData(data []byte, secret *ciphersuite.Secret) ([]byte, error) {
	// Derive key and nonce from secret
	// sender_data_key = ExpandWithLabel(sender_data_secret, "key", "", key_length)
	// sender_data_nonce = ExpandWithLabel(sender_data_secret, "nonce", "", nonce_length)
	key := make([]byte, 16)
	nonce := make([]byte, 12)

	return pm.encryptWithAESGCM(data, key, nonce, nil)
}

// decryptSenderData decrypts sender data.
func (pm *PrivateMessage) decryptSenderData(data []byte, secret *ciphersuite.Secret) ([]byte, error) {
	key := make([]byte, 16)
	nonce := make([]byte, 12)

	return pm.decryptWithAESGCM(data, key, nonce, nil)
}

// computeAAD computes the authenticated data for content encryption.
func (pm *PrivateMessage) computeAAD() []byte {
	w := tls.NewWriter()

	// Wire format
	w.WriteUint16(uint16(WireFormatPrivateMessage))

	// Group ID
	w.WriteVLBytes(pm.GroupID.AsSlice())

	// Epoch
	w.WriteUint64(pm.Epoch.AsUint64())

	// Content type
	w.WriteUint8(uint8(pm.ContentType))

	// Authenticated data
	w.WriteVLBytes(pm.AuthenticatedData)

	// Encrypted sender data
	w.WriteVLBytes(pm.EncryptedSenderData)

	return w.Bytes()
}

// encryptWithAESGCM encrypts data using AES-GCM.
func (pm *PrivateMessage) encryptWithAESGCM(plaintext, key, nonce, aad []byte) ([]byte, error) {
	block, err := aes.NewCipher(key)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	aead, err := cipher.NewGCM(block)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	return aead.Seal(nil, nonce, plaintext, aad), nil
}

// decryptWithAESGCM decrypts data using AES-GCM.
func (pm *PrivateMessage) decryptWithAESGCM(ciphertext, key, nonce, aad []byte) ([]byte, error) {
	block, err := aes.NewCipher(key)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	aead, err := cipher.NewGCM(block)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	return aead.Open(nil, nonce, ciphertext, aad)
}
```

## 5. framing/mls_message.go

```go
package framing

import (
	"fmt"

	"github.com/openmls/go/group"
	"github.com/openmls/go/internal/tls"
	"github.com/openmls/go/keypackages"
)

// MLSMessage represents a generic MLS message on the wire.
//
// This is the top-level message type that can be any of the MLS message types.
type MLSMessage struct {
	Version uint16 // Protocol version
	Body    MLSMessageBody
}

// MLSMessageBody represents the body of an MLS message.
type MLSMessageBody struct {
	// Only one of these should be set
	PublicMessage  *PublicMessage
	PrivateMessage *PrivateMessage
	Welcome        *group.Welcome
	GroupInfo      *group.GroupInfo
	KeyPackage     *keypackages.KeyPackage
}

// WireFormat returns the wire format of the message.
func (m *MLSMessage) WireFormat() WireFormat {
	switch {
	case m.Body.PublicMessage != nil:
		return WireFormatPublicMessage
	case m.Body.PrivateMessage != nil:
		return WireFormatPrivateMessage
	case m.Body.Welcome != nil:
		return WireFormatWelcome
	case m.Body.GroupInfo != nil:
		return WireFormatGroupInfo
	case m.Body.KeyPackage != nil:
		return WireFormatKeyPackage
	default:
		return 0
	}
}

// Marshal serializes the MLSMessage to TLS format.
func (m *MLSMessage) Marshal() []byte {
	w := tls.NewWriter()

	// Version
	w.WriteUint16(m.Version)

	// Wire format
	w.WriteUint16(uint16(m.WireFormat()))

	// Body
	switch m.WireFormat() {
	case WireFormatPublicMessage:
		w.WriteRaw(m.Body.PublicMessage.Marshal())
	case WireFormatPrivateMessage:
		w.WriteRaw(m.Body.PrivateMessage.Marshal())
	case WireFormatWelcome:
		w.WriteRaw(m.Body.Welcome.Marshal())
	case WireFormatGroupInfo:
		// TODO: Implement GroupInfo serialization
		w.WriteVLBytes([]byte{})
	case WireFormatKeyPackage:
		w.WriteRaw(m.Body.KeyPackage.Marshal())
	}

	return w.Bytes()
}

// UnmarshalMLSMessage deserializes an MLSMessage from TLS format.
func UnmarshalMLSMessage(data []byte) (*MLSMessage, error) {
	r := tls.NewReader(data)

	// Version
	version, err := r.ReadUint16()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("reading version: %w", err)
	}

	// Wire format
	wireFormat, err := r.ReadUint16()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("reading wire format: %w", err)
	}

	msg := &MLSMessage{
		Version: version,
	}

	// Read remaining data as body
	bodyData := r.BytesAfterPosition()

	switch WireFormat(wireFormat) {
	case WireFormatPublicMessage:
		pm, err := UnmarshalPublicMessage(bodyData)
		if err != nil {
			return nil, fmt.Errorf("unmarshaling public message: %w", err)
		}
		msg.Body = MLSMessageBody{PublicMessage: pm}

	case WireFormatPrivateMessage:
		pm, err := UnmarshalPrivateMessage(bodyData)
		if err != nil {
			return nil, fmt.Errorf("unmarshaling private message: %w", err)
		}
		msg.Body = MLSMessageBody{PrivateMessage: pm}

	case WireFormatWelcome:
		// TODO: Implement Welcome deserialization
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("welcome deserialization not implemented")

	case WireFormatGroupInfo:
		// TODO: Implement GroupInfo deserialization
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("groupinfo deserialization not implemented")

	case WireFormatKeyPackage:
		kp, err := keypackages.UnmarshalKeyPackage(bodyData)
		if err != nil {
			return nil, fmt.Errorf("unmarshaling key package: %w", err)
		}
		msg.Body = MLSMessageBody{KeyPackage: kp}

	default:
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("unknown wire format: %d", wireFormat)
	}

	return msg, nil
}

// NewPublicMLSMessage creates a new MLS message containing a public message.
func NewPublicMLSMessage(pm *PublicMessage) *MLSMessage {
	return &MLSMessage{
		Version: 1, // MLS 1.0
		Body:    MLSMessageBody{PublicMessage: pm},
	}
}

// NewPrivateMLSMessage creates a new MLS message containing a private message.
func NewPrivateMLSMessage(pm *PrivateMessage) *MLSMessage {
	return &MLSMessage{
		Version: 1, // MLS 1.0
		Body:    MLSMessageBody{PrivateMessage: pm},
	}
}
```

## 6. framing/errors.go

```go
package framing

import "fmt"

// FramingError represents framing-related errors.
type FramingError string

const (
	ErrInvalidWireFormat    FramingError = "invalid wire format"
	ErrInvalidContentType   FramingError = "invalid content type"
	ErrInvalidSenderType    FramingError = "invalid sender type"
	ErrDecryptionFailed     FramingError = "decryption failed"
	ErrVerificationFailed   FramingError = "signature verification failed"
	ErrInvalidMessage       FramingError = "invalid message"
	ErrSerializationFailed  FramingError = "serialization failed"
	ErrDeserializationFailed FramingError = "deserialization failed"
)

func (e FramingError) Error() string {
	return string(e)
}

// NewFramingError creates a new framing error with context.
func NewFramingError(err FramingError, context string) error {
	return fmt.Errorf("%s: %s", err, context)
}
```

## 7. framing/framing_test.go

```go
package framing

import (
	"bytes"
	"testing"

	"github.com/openmls/go/ciphersuite"
	"github.com/openmls/go/group"
)

func TestSenderTypes(t *testing.T) {
	// Test member sender
	memberSender := NewMemberSender(group.NewLeafNodeIndex(5))
	if !memberSender.IsMember() {
		t.Error("Expected member sender")
	}
	if memberSender.IsExternal() {
		t.Error("Should not be external")
	}

	// Test external sender
	extSender := NewExternalSender(1)
	if !extSender.IsExternal() {
		t.Error("Expected external sender")
	}
	if extSender.IsMember() {
		t.Error("Should not be member")
	}

	// Test new member senders
	newMemberProp := NewNewMemberProposalSender()
	if !newMemberProp.IsNewMember() {
		t.Error("Expected new member sender")
	}

	newMemberCommit := NewNewMemberCommitSender()
	if !newMemberCommit.IsNewMember() {
		t.Error("Expected new member sender")
	}
}

func TestSenderMarshalUnmarshal(t *testing.T) {
	testCases := []struct {
		name   string
		sender *Sender
	}{
		{"Member", NewMemberSender(group.NewLeafNodeIndex(42))},
		{"External", NewExternalSender(7)},
		{"NewMemberProposal", NewNewMemberProposalSender()},
		{"NewMemberCommit", NewNewMemberCommitSender()},
	}

	for _, tc := range testCases {
		t.Run(tc.name, func(t *testing.T) {
			data := tc.sender.Marshal()
			if len(data) == 0 {
				t.Fatal("Marshal returned empty data")
			}

			sender2, err := UnmarshalSender(data)
			if err != nil {
				t.Fatalf("Unmarshal failed: %v", err)
			}

			if sender2.Type != tc.sender.Type {
				t.Errorf("Type mismatch: %d vs %d", sender2.Type, tc.sender.Type)
			}

			if tc.sender.Type == SenderTypeMember && sender2.LeafIndex != tc.sender.LeafIndex {
				t.Errorf("LeafIndex mismatch")
			}
		})
	}
}

func TestContentTypes(t *testing.T) {
	types := []ContentType{
		ContentTypeApplication,
		ContentTypeProposal,
		ContentTypeCommit,
	}

	for _, ct := range types {
		if ct < 1 || ct > 3 {
			t.Errorf("Invalid content type: %d", ct)
		}
	}
}

func TestWireFormats(t *testing.T) {
	formats := []WireFormat{
		WireFormatPublicMessage,
		WireFormatPrivateMessage,
		WireFormatWelcome,
		WireFormatGroupInfo,
		WireFormatKeyPackage,
	}

	for _, wf := range formats {
		if wf < 1 || wf > 5 {
			t.Errorf("Invalid wire format: %d", wf)
		}
	}
}

func TestPublicMessageMarshal(t *testing.T) {
	content := &FramedContent{
		GroupID:     group.NewGroupID([]byte("test_group")),
		Epoch:       group.NewGroupEpoch(5),
		Sender:      NewMemberSender(group.NewLeafNodeIndex(0)),
		ContentType: ContentTypeApplication,
		Body:        FramedContentBody{ApplicationData: []byte("hello")},
	}

	pm := NewPublicMessage(content)
	sig := ciphersuite.NewSignature([]byte("test_signature"))
	pm.SetSignature(sig)

	data := pm.Marshal()
	if len(data) == 0 {
		t.Fatal("Marshal returned empty data")
	}

	pm2, err := UnmarshalPublicMessage(data)
	if err != nil {
		t.Fatalf("Unmarshal failed: %v", err)
	}

	if pm2.Content.Epoch != content.Epoch {
		t.Errorf("Epoch mismatch")
	}

	if !bytes.Equal(pm2.Signature.AsSlice(), sig.AsSlice()) {
		t.Error("Signature mismatch")
	}
}

func TestPrivateMessageMarshal(t *testing.T) {
	pm := NewPrivateMessage(
		group.NewGroupID([]byte("test_group")),
		group.NewGroupEpoch(5),
		ContentTypeApplication,
	)

	pm.SetAuthenticatedData([]byte("aad"))
	pm.SetEncryptedSenderData([]byte("encrypted_sender"))
	pm.SetCiphertext([]byte("encrypted_content"))

	data := pm.Marshal()
	if len(data) == 0 {
		t.Fatal("Marshal returned empty data")
	}

	pm2, err := UnmarshalPrivateMessage(data)
	if err != nil {
		t.Fatalf("Unmarshal failed: %v", err)
	}

	if pm2.Epoch != pm.Epoch {
		t.Errorf("Epoch mismatch")
	}

	if !bytes.Equal(pm2.Ciphertext, pm.Ciphertext) {
		t.Error("Ciphertext mismatch")
	}
}

func TestMLSMessage(t *testing.T) {
	content := &FramedContent{
		GroupID:     group.NewGroupID([]byte("test_group")),
		Epoch:       group.NewGroupEpoch(1),
		Sender:      NewMemberSender(group.NewLeafNodeIndex(0)),
		ContentType: ContentTypeApplication,
		Body:        FramedContentBody{ApplicationData: []byte("hello")},
	}

	pm := NewPublicMessage(content)
	msg := NewPublicMLSMessage(pm)

	if msg.WireFormat() != WireFormatPublicMessage {
		t.Errorf("Expected PublicMessage wire format, got %d", msg.WireFormat())
	}

	data := msg.Marshal()
	if len(data) == 0 {
		t.Fatal("Marshal returned empty data")
	}

	msg2, err := UnmarshalMLSMessage(data)
	if err != nil {
		t.Fatalf("Unmarshal failed: %v", err)
	}

	if msg2.WireFormat() != WireFormatPublicMessage {
		t.Error("Wire format mismatch after unmarshal")
	}
}

func TestFramedContentBody(t *testing.T) {
	// Test application data
	appData := []byte("hello world")
	body := NewApplicationContent(appData)
	if !bytes.Equal(body.ApplicationData, appData) {
		t.Error("Application data mismatch")
	}

	// Test proposal content
	proposal := &group.Proposal{Type: group.ProposalTypeAdd}
	body = NewProposalContent(proposal)
	if body.Proposal == nil {
		t.Error("Proposal should not be nil")
	}

	// Test commit content
	commit := &group.Commit{}
	body = NewCommitContent(commit)
	if body.Commit == nil {
		t.Error("Commit should not be nil")
	}
}

func TestSenderDataMarshal(t *testing.T) {
	pm := &PrivateMessage{}

	sd := &SenderData{
		LeafIndex:  group.NewLeafNodeIndex(5),
		Generation: 42,
		ReuseGuard: [4]byte{0x01, 0x02, 0x03, 0x04},
	}

	data := pm.marshalSenderData(sd)
	if len(data) != 12 {
		t.Errorf("Expected 12 bytes, got %d", len(data))
	}

	sd2, err := pm.unmarshalSenderData(data)
	if err != nil {
		t.Fatalf("Unmarshal failed: %v", err)
	}

	if sd2.LeafIndex != sd.LeafIndex {
		t.Error("LeafIndex mismatch")
	}

	if sd2.Generation != sd.Generation {
		t.Error("Generation mismatch")
	}

	if sd2.ReuseGuard != sd.ReuseGuard {
		t.Error("ReuseGuard mismatch")
	}
}

func TestPublicMessageTranscriptHash(t *testing.T) {
	content := &FramedContent{
		GroupID:     group.NewGroupID([]byte("test")),
		Epoch:       group.NewGroupEpoch(1),
		Sender:      NewMemberSender(group.NewLeafNodeIndex(0)),
		ContentType: ContentTypeCommit,
	}

	pm := NewPublicMessage(content)

	// Test confirmed transcript hash input
	input := pm.ConfirmedTranscriptHashInput()
	if len(input) == 0 {
		t.Error("ConfirmedTranscriptHashInput returned empty data")
	}

	// Test interim transcript hash input
	interimInput := pm.InterimTranscriptHashInput([]byte("confirmation_tag"))
	if len(interimInput) == 0 {
		t.Error("InterimTranscriptHashInput returned empty data")
	}
}

func TestPrivateMessageAAD(t *testing.T) {
	pm := NewPrivateMessage(
		group.NewGroupID([]byte("test_group")),
		group.NewGroupEpoch(5),
		ContentTypeApplication,
	)
	pm.SetAuthenticatedData([]byte("authenticated_data"))
	pm.SetEncryptedSenderData([]byte("sender_data"))

	aad := pm.computeAAD()
	if len(aad) == 0 {
		t.Error("computeAAD returned empty data")
	}

	// AAD should include all public fields
	if !bytes.Contains(aad, []byte("test_group")) {
		t.Error("AAD should contain group_id")
	}
}
```

2. We've implemented the schedule package (Key Schedule)

The user wants me to provide code for the framing package and then verify everything works. But first, they want a summary of what we've done so far.

Let me create a comprehensive summary following the template provided.

---
## Goal

Implement a complete Go port of the OpenMLS Rust implementation for the Messaging Layer Security (MLS) Protocol (RFC 9420), specifically focusing on cryptographic primitives, key schedule, group management, and message framing. The implementation must be compatible with the DAVE (Discord Audio/Video End-to-end Encryption) protocol.

## Instructions

- **Port from Rust to Go**: Convert OpenMLS Rust code idiomatically to Go
- **Follow RFC 9420**: All implementations must strictly follow RFC 9420 specifications
- **DAVE Protocol Support**: Must support DAVE protocol requirements (DHKEMP256_AES128GCM_SHA256_P256 ciphersuite)
- **Code-First Approach**: User wants to receive code only, then verify it works
- **Test Coverage**: All packages must have comprehensive tests that pass
- **Type Safety**: Handle type conversions between packages carefully (notably `ciphersuite.CipherSuite` vs `keypackages.CipherSuite`)

## Discoveries

- **Type Mismatch Issues**: Found conflicts between `ciphersuite.CipherSuite` (uint16) and `keypackages.CipherSuite` (uint16) - both define the same constant but are different types in Go. Fixed by explicit casting.
- **KeyPackageRef Functions**: `MakeKeyPackageRef` and `MakeProposalRef` are in `ciphersuite` package, not `keypackages`.
- **Private Key Handling**: `KeyPackagePrivateKeys.InitKey` is `*ecdh.PrivateKey`, needs `.Bytes()` call for serialization.
- **HKDF Implementation**: Created shared `hkdf.go` to avoid duplicate function definitions between `secret.go` and `hpke.go`.
- **Test Dependencies**: Tests reveal integration issues between packages that static analysis doesn't catch (e.g., ProposalRemove test needed commit+merge before member existed).

## Accomplished

### ✅ Completed Packages:

1. **ciphersuite/** (11 files, 19 tests) - All tests passing
   - Core cryptographic primitives (AES-128-GCM, ECDSA P-256, SHA-256)
   - HPKE encryption (DHKEM P-256)
   - HKDF key derivation
   - Secret management with secure zeroing
   - Hash references (KeyPackageRef, ProposalRef)
   - AEAD encryption/decryption
   - Signatures and verification
   - Reuse guards for nonce protection

2. **schedule/** (4 files, 7 tests) - All tests passing
   - Key Schedule state machine (Initial → Context → Done)
   - All epoch secrets derivation (init, sender_data, encryption, exporter, authentication, external, confirm, membership, resumption)
   - PSK handling (External and Resumption)
   - MLS Exporter for DAVE protocol
   - Welcome secret computation

3. **group/** (9 files, 9 tests) - All tests passing
   - Group creation and joining
   - GroupContext (RFC 9420 §8.1)
   - Proposal handling (Add, Update, Remove, PreSharedKey)
   - Commit creation and merging
   - Welcome message handling
   - Member management
   - Ratchet tree operations (basic)
   - Epoch advancement

4. **framing/** (7 files, ~12 tests) - Code provided, needs implementation
   - PublicMessage (signed, unencrypted) - RFC 9420 §6.2
   - PrivateMessage (encrypted) - RFC 9420 §6.3
   - Sender types (Member, External, NewMember)
   - Content types (Application, Proposal, Commit)
   - FramedContent structure
   - WireFormat handling
   - MLSMessage wrapper

### 🔄 In Progress:
- Creating framing package files (code provided, needs to be written to disk)
- Running tests to verify framing package

```
8: // Commit represents an MLS Commit message (RFC 9420 §12.4).

61: func (c *Commit) Marshal() []byte {
62: 	w := tls.NewWriter()
63: 	// Proposals
64: 	propBuf := tls.NewWriter()
65: 	for _, por := range c.Proposals {
66: 		if por.Proposal != nil {
67: 			// Serialize proposal (simplified)
68: 			propBuf.WriteUint8(0x01) // Proposal present
69: 		} else {
70: 			propBuf.WriteVLBytes(por.ProposalRef)
71: 		}
72: 	}
73: 	w.WriteVLBytes(propBuf.Bytes())
74: 	// Path (optional)
75: 	if c.Path != nil {
76: 		w.WriteUint8(0x01)
77: 		// Serialize path (simplified)
78: 	} else {
```

```json
  "oldString": "\treturn w.Bytes()\n}",
  "newString": "\treturn w.Bytes()\n}\n\n// UnmarshalCommit deserializes a Commit from TLS format.\nfunc UnmarshalCommit(data []byte) (*Commit, error) {\n\tr := tls.NewReader(data)\n\t\n\tcommit := &Commit{\n\t\tProposals: make([]ProposalOrRef, 0),\n\t}\n\t\n\t// Read proposals (variable-length vector)\n\tproposalsData, err := r.ReadVLBytes()\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\t\n\tif len(proposalsData) > 0 {\n\t\tpropReader := tls.NewReader(proposalsData)\n\t\tfor propReader.Len() > 0 {\n\t\t\t// Read proposal type/indicator\n\t\t\tpropType, err := propReader.ReadUint8()\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\tif propType == 0x01 {\n\t\t\t\t// Proposal present (simplified - full deserialization would need Proposal type)\n\t\t\t\t// For now, skip the proposal data\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t// ProposalRef\n\t\t\t\tref, err := propReader.ReadVLBytes()\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tcommit.Proposals = append(commit.Proposals, ProposalOrRef{\n\t\t\t\t\tProposalRef: ref,\n\t\t\t\t})\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\t\n\t// Read optional path\n\tpathPresent, err := r.ReadUint8()\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\t\n\tif pathPresent == 0x01 {\n\t\t// Path is present (simplified - would need full UpdatePath deserialization)\n\t\tcommit.Path = &UpdatePath{}\n\t}\n\t\n\treturn commit, nil\n}"
}
```

```
<path>/home/enano/butakero-bot-service/openmls-go/internal/tls/tls.go</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: // Package tls implements TLS presentation language encoding/decoding.
2: //
3: // This is a minimal implementation of RFC 8446 §3 for MLS message encoding.
4: // It's based on the tls_codec Rust crate used by OpenMLS.
5: package tls
6: 
7: import (
8: 	"encoding/binary"
9: 	"errors"
10: 	"fmt"
11: )
12: 
13: // Writer writes TLS presentation language format.
14: type Writer struct {
15: 	buf []byte
16: }
17: 
18: // NewWriter creates a new TLS writer.
19: func NewWriter() *Writer {
20: 	return &Writer{
21: 		buf: make([]byte, 0, 256),
22: 	}
23: }
24: 
25: // Bytes returns the written bytes.
26: func (w *Writer) Bytes() []byte {
27: 	return w.buf
28: }
29: 
30: // WriteUint8 writes an 8-bit unsigned integer.
31: func (w *Writer) WriteUint8(v uint8) {
32: 	w.buf = append(w.buf, v)
33: }
34: 
35: // WriteUint16 writes a 16-bit unsigned integer in big-endian.
36: func (w *Writer) WriteUint16(v uint16) {
37: 	w.buf = append(w.buf, byte(v>>8), byte(v))
38: }
39: 
40: // WriteUint32 writes a 32-bit unsigned integer in big-endian.
41: func (w *Writer) WriteUint32(v uint32) {
42: 	w.buf = append(w.buf, byte(v>>24), byte(v>>16), byte(v>>8), byte(v))
43: }
44: 
45: // WriteUint64 writes a 64-bit unsigned integer in big-endian.
46: func (w *Writer) WriteUint64(v uint64) {
47: 	w.buf = append(w.buf,
48: 		byte(v>>56), byte(v>>48), byte(v>>40), byte(v>>32),
49: 		byte(v>>24), byte(v>>16), byte(v>>8), byte(v),
50: 	)
51: }
52: 
53: // WriteVLBytes writes a variable-length byte vector.
54: //
55: // Format: length<V> || data
56: // where length is encoded as ULEB128
57: func (w *Writer) WriteVLBytes(data []byte) {
58: 	w.WriteULEB128(uint32(len(data)))
59: 	w.buf = append(w.buf, data...)
60: }
61: 
62: // WriteRaw writes raw bytes without encoding.
63: func (w *Writer) WriteRaw(data []byte) {
64: 	w.buf = append(w.buf, data...)
65: }
66: 
67: // WriteULEB128 writes an unsigned integer in ULEB128 format.
68: func (w *Writer) WriteULEB128(v uint32) {
69: 	for v >= 0x80 {
70: 		w.buf = append(w.buf, byte(v)|0x80)
71: 		v >>= 7
72: 	}
73: 	w.buf = append(w.buf, byte(v))
74: }
75: 
76: // Reader reads TLS presentation language format.
77: type Reader struct {
78: 	buf []byte
79: 	pos int
80: }
81: 
82: // NewReader creates a new TLS reader.
83: func NewReader(data []byte) *Reader {
84: 	return &Reader{
85: 		buf: data,
86: 		pos: 0,
87: 	}
88: }
89: 
90: // Remaining returns the number of unread bytes.
91: func (r *Reader) Remaining() int {
92: 	return len(r.buf) - r.pos
93: }
94: 
95: // Position returns the current read position.
96: func (r *Reader) Position() int {
97: 	return r.pos
98: }
99: 
100: // SetPosition sets the read position.
101: func (r *Reader) SetPosition(pos int) {
102: 	r.pos = pos
103: }
104: 
105: // Skip advances the position by n bytes.
106: func (r *Reader) Skip(n int) {
107: 	r.pos += n
108: }
109: 
110: // BytesAfterPosition returns bytes from current position to end.
111: func (r *Reader) BytesAfterPosition() []byte {
112: 	return r.buf[r.pos:]
113: }
114: 
115: // ReadUint8 reads an 8-bit unsigned integer.
116: func (r *Reader) ReadUint8() (uint8, error) {
117: 	if r.pos >= len(r.buf) {
118: 		return 0, errors.New("buffer underrun")
119: 	}
120: 	v := r.buf[r.pos]
121: 	r.pos++
122: 	return v, nil
123: }
124: 
125: // ReadUint16 reads a 16-bit unsigned integer in big-endian.
126: func (r *Reader) ReadUint16() (uint16, error) {
127: 	if r.pos+2 > len(r.buf) {
128: 		return 0, errors.New("buffer underrun")
129: 	}
130: 	v := binary.BigEndian.Uint16(r.buf[r.pos:])
131: 	r.pos += 2
132: 	return v, nil
133: }
134: 
135: // ReadUint32 reads a 32-bit unsigned integer in big-endian.
136: func (r *Reader) ReadUint32() (uint32, error) {
137: 	if r.pos+4 > len(r.buf) {
138: 		return 0, errors.New("buffer underrun")
139: 	}
140: 	v := binary.BigEndian.Uint32(r.buf[r.pos:])
141: 	r.pos += 4
142: 	return v, nil
143: }
144: 
145: // ReadUint64 reads a 64-bit unsigned integer in big-endian.
146: func (r *Reader) ReadUint64() (uint64, error) {
147: 	if r.pos+8 > len(r.buf) {
148: 		return 0, errors.New("buffer underrun")
149: 	}
150: 	v := binary.BigEndian.Uint64(r.buf[r.pos:])
151: 	r.pos += 8
152: 	return v, nil
153: }
154: 
155: // ReadVLBytes reads a variable-length byte vector.
156: func (r *Reader) ReadVLBytes() ([]byte, error) {
157: 	length, err := r.ReadULEB128()
158: 	if err != nil {
159: 		return nil, err
160: 	}
161: 
162: 	if r.pos+int(length) > len(r.buf) {
163: 		return nil, fmt.Errorf("buffer underrun: need %d bytes, have %d", length, r.Remaining())
164: 	}
165: 
166: 	data := make([]byte, length)
167: 	copy(data, r.buf[r.pos:r.pos+int(length)])
168: 	r.pos += int(length)
169: 
170: 	return data, nil
171: }
172: 
173: // ReadULEB128 reads an unsigned integer in ULEB128 format.
174: func (r *Reader) ReadULEB128() (uint32, error) {
175: 	var result uint32
176: 	var shift uint
177: 
178: 	for {
179: 		if r.pos >= len(r.buf) {
180: 			return 0, errors.New("buffer underrun")
181: 		}
182: 
183: 		b := r.buf[r.pos]
184: 		r.pos++
185: 
186: 		result |= uint32(b&0x7F) << shift
187: 		if b&0x80 == 0 {
188: 			break
189: 		}
190: 
191: 		shift += 7
192: 		if shift >= 32 {
193: 			return 0, errors.New("ULEB128 overflow")
194: 		}
195: 	}
196: 
197: 	return result, nil
198: }
199: 
200: // ReadBytes reads n bytes.
201: func (r *Reader) ReadBytes(n int) ([]byte, error) {
202: 	if r.pos+n > len(r.buf) {
203: 		return nil, errors.New("buffer underrun")
204: 	}
205: 
206: 	data := make([]byte, n)
207: 	copy(data, r.buf[r.pos:r.pos+n])
208: 	r.pos += n
209: 
210: 	return data, nil
211: }

(End of file - total 211 lines)
</content>
```

## Assistant (Build · k2p5 · 5.4s)

_Thinking:_

The `Reader` has a `Remaining()` method, not `Len()`. I need to update the commit.go file to use `Remaining()` instead.

**Tool: edit**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "filePath": "/home/enano/butakero-bot-service/openmls-go/group/commit.go",
  "oldString": "\tif len(proposalsData) > 0 {\n\t\tpropReader := tls.NewReader(proposalsData)\n\t\tfor propReader.Len() > 0 {",
  "newString": "\tif len(proposalsData) > 0 {\n\t\tpropReader := tls.NewReader(proposalsData)\n\t\tfor propReader.Remaining() > 0 {"
}
```

**Output:**
```
Edit applied successfully.
```

```
53: 	// Content
```

## Assistant (Build · k2p5 · 8.2s)

_Thinking:_

Ahora entiendo los problemas:

1. **Error de unmarshaling**: En `UnmarshalFramedContent`, el problema está en la lectura del `Sender`. El código está usando `r.BytesAfterPosition()` para obtener los datos del sender y luego usar `len(sender.Marshal())` para saltar esos bytes, pero esto es problemático porque `UnmarshalSender` puede consumir datos de forma diferente a como los serializa `Marshal()`.

2. **Panic nil pointer**: En `FramedContent.Marshal()` línea 74, cuando `ContentType` es `ContentTypeCommit`, llama a `fc.Body.Commit.Marshal()` pero si `Commit` es nil, esto causa un panic.

3. **Error de unmarshaling (2)**: En `UnmarshalPublicMessage`, la línea 83 `contentData, err := r.ReadVLBytes()` está intentando leer el contenido como un vector de longitud variable, pero en `Marshal()` de `FramedContent`, el contenido se escribe directamente sin envolverlo en un vector de longitud variable primero.

Veamos el test para entender mejor:

**Tool: read**

```json

  "filePath": "/home/enano/butakero-bot-service/openmls-go/framing/framing_test.go"
```

## Assistant (Build · k2p5 · 14.6s)

_Thinking:_

Ahora entiendo los problemas:

1. **TestPublicMessageMarshal**: El problema es en `UnmarshalPublicMessage` que espera leer el contenido como `ReadVLBytes()` pero en `Marshal()` el contenido se escribe directamente sin el prefijo de longitud variable. En el Marshal de PublicMessage línea 54: `w.WriteRaw(pm.Content.Marshal())` - esto escribe el contenido directamente sin envolverlo en un vector de longitud variable. Pero en UnmarshalPublicMessage línea 83: `contentData, err := r.ReadVLBytes()` - esto espera leer un vector de longitud variable.

2. **TestPublicMessageTranscriptHash**: El panic ocurre en línea 222 cuando `ContentType` es `ContentTypeCommit` pero el `Body.Commit` es nil. En `FramedContent.Marshal()` línea 74 se llama a `fc.Body.Commit.Marshal()` sin verificar si `Commit` es nil.

Los problemas son:
1. Inconsistencia entre Marshal y Unmarshal en PublicMessage (con/sin VLBytes wrapper)
2. Nil pointer cuando Commit es nil en FramedContent.Marshal()

Voy a arreglar ambos problemas.

Ahora entiendo los problemas. Hay 2 errores:

1. **Inconsistencia Marshal/Unmarshal**: En `PublicMessage.Marshal()` el contenido se escribe directamente (`WriteRaw`), pero en `UnmarshalPublicMessage()` se intenta leer como `ReadVLBytes()`
2. **Nil pointer**: Cuando `ContentType` es `Commit` pero `Body.Commit` es nil, se produce un panic

Voy a corregir:

**Tool: edit**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "filePath": "/home/enano/butakero-bot-service/openmls-go/framing/public_message.go",
  "oldString": "// Marshal serializes the PublicMessage to TLS format.\nfunc (pm *PublicMessage) Marshal() []byte {\n\tw := tls.NewWriter()\n\t// Wire format\n\tw.WriteUint16(uint16(WireFormatPublicMessage))\n\t// Content\n\tw.WriteRaw(pm.Content.Marshal())",
  "newString": "// Marshal serializes the PublicMessage to TLS format.\nfunc (pm *PublicMessage) Marshal() []byte {\n\tw := tls.NewWriter()\n\t// Wire format\n\tw.WriteUint16(uint16(WireFormatPublicMessage))\n\t// Content (as variable-length bytes)\n\tw.WriteVLBytes(pm.Content.Marshal())"
}
```

**Output:**
```
Edit applied successfully.
```

## Assistant (Plan · k2p5 · 20.2s)

_Thinking:_

Ahora tengo una buena comprensión del estado actual. El plan es muy completo y mejora significativamente el código actual. Mis comentarios:

1. **Excelente plan** - Aborda problemas reales de seguridad y compatibilidad
2. **Mejoras necesarias**:
   - Múltiples cipher suites (actualmente solo 0x0002)
   - HKDF manual → crypto/hkdf (mejor seguridad)
   - DER encoding consistente para firmas
   - HPKE completo con circl
   - runtime.KeepAlive para secrets
   - Error wrapping moderno

3. **Dependencia circl**: Justificada, Go no tiene API pública de HPKE

4. **Timeline**: Es un cambio grande, podría romper compatibilidad temporalmente

Debo preguntar si quiere proceder y si quiere hacerlo en partes o todo de una vez.

**Mi opinión sobre el plan:**

El plan es **excelente** y aborda problemas críticos reales:

✅ **Pros:**
- Múltiples cipher suites necesarios para interoperabilidad con openmls Rust
- `crypto/hkdf` es definitivamente mejor que implementación manual (audited, optimizado)
- DER encoding consistente requerido por RFC 9420 §5.1.2
- circl es la única opción viable para HPKE (Go no tiene API pública)
- `runtime.KeepAlive()` en puntos críticos mejora seguridad sin overkill
- Error wrapping moderno facilita debugging

⚠️ **Consideraciones:**
- **Breaking changes**: Cambiará APIs existentes (ej: HKDF, signatures)
- **Nueva dependencia**: `github.com/cloudflare/circl` (~1MB)
- **Timeline**: Son ~7 archivos nuevos/modificados, trabajo sustancial

**Preguntas antes de proceder:**

1. ¿Quieres implementar **todo el plan de una vez** o **por partes** (ej: primero HKDF, luego cipher suites, etc.)?

2. ¿Es aceptable agregar la dependencia `circl`? (es la única opción para HPKE completo)

3. ¿Hay alguna parte específica que quieras **omitir** o **priorizar**?

4. ¿Quieres mantener **compatibilidad hacia atrás** o puede haber breaking changes?

Dime cómo proceder y empiezo la implementación.

## 📋 Plan de Implementación por Partes

He dividido el plan en **8 milestones** para commits pequeños y manejables:

### **Parte 1: Foundation** 
- Crear `errors.go` con errores específicos y wrapping (`fmt.Errorf("%w")`)
- Modificar `ciphersuite.go`: agregar 3 cipher suites (0x0001, 0x0002, 0x0003)
- Agregar `CipherSuiteParams`, registry pattern, métodos auxiliares (`HashLength()`, `AEADKeyLength()`, etc.)

### **Parte 2: HKDF Modernization**
- Reemplazar `hkdf.go`: eliminar implementación manual, usar `crypto/hkdf`
- Agregar `runtime.KeepAlive()` en Extract/Expand
- Tests con RFC 5869 test vectors

### **Parte 3: Signature DER Encoding**
- Modificar `signature.go`: unificar todo a DER encoding (ECDSA)
- Agregar funciones `SignWithScheme`/`VerifyWithScheme`
- Agregar `runtime.KeepAlive()` para private keys
- Soporte Ed25519 nativo

### **Parte 4: HPKE with circl**
- Actualizar `go.mod`: agregar `github.com/cloudflare/circl v1.3.7`
- Reescribir `hpke.go`: implementación completa con circl
- Implementar `EncryptWithLabel`/`DecryptWithLabel` (RFC 9420 §5.1.3)
- Tests con round-trip encryption

### **Parte 5: Secret Management**
- Modificar `secret.go`: agregar `runtime.KeepAlive()` selectivo
- Integrar con nuevo HKDF
- `SecureZero()` con KeepAlive para prevenir optimización

### **Parte 6: Crypto Provider Interface**
- Crear `provider.go`: `CryptoProvider` interface
- Implementar `StdCryptoProvider`
- Funciones globales `SetProvider()`/`GetProvider()`

### **Parte 7: go.mod Update**
- Agregar dependencia circl
- `go mod tidy`

### **Parte 8: Test Updates**
- Actualizar tests existentes para breaking changes
- Asegurar que todos los tests pasen

---

**¿Te parece bien este orden? ¿Quieres que empiece con la Parte 1?**

Cada parte será un commit separado que puedes revisar antes de continuar con la siguiente.
